<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:распорядиться.html>распоряди́ться</a> (4646)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рядить.html>ряди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распорядиться.html>распоряди́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasporjadítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распоряжаться.html>распоряжа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to order, to make arrangements, to see to it (that)</li>
<li>to deal (with), to handle</li></ol>

***расправа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расправа.html>распра́ва</a> (8257)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправа.html>распра́ва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspráva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправа.html>распра́вы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправа.html>распра́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправа.html>распра́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>massacre, carnage</li>
<li><i>(savage)</i> punishment (of), harsh treatment (of), reprisals (against), violence
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1928–1940</b>,  Михаил Александрович Шолохов (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mikhail_Aleksandrovich_Sholokhov" class="extiw" title="w:Mikhail Aleksandrovich Sholokhov">Mikhail Aleksandrovich Sholokhov</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:тихий.html>Ти́хий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дно.html>Дон</a></cite>, Book 3, Part 6, Chapter 36 |  translated as Robert Daglish; Brian Murphy, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/And_Quiet_Flows_the_Don" class="extiw" title="w:And Quiet Flows the Don">Quiet Flows the Don</a></cite>, Carroll amp; Graf, 1996, page 810:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">«<a href = vnd.unilang:многоуважаемый.html>многоуважа́емый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:товарищ.html>това́рищ</a> григо́рий пантеле́евич! <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>До</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́шего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сведение.html>све́дения</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:коварный.html>кова́рные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доходить.html>дохо́дят</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слух.html>слу́хи</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:якобы.html>я́кобы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учинять.html>учиня́ешь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жестокий.html>жесто́кую</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:расправа.html>распра́ву</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пленный.html>пле́нными</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:красноармеец.html>красноарме́йцами</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:будто.html>бу́дто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>твоему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приказ.html>прика́зу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уничтоженный.html>уничто́жены</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сиречь.html>си́речь</a> порубаны — <a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>три́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:красноармеец.html>красноарме́йцев</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:взятый.html>взя́тые</a> Харлампием Ермаковым <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> бо́ковской. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>»</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">“Mnogouvažájemyj továrišč Grigórij Panteléjevič! Do náševo svédenija kovárnyje doxódjat slúxi, jákoby ty učinjáješʹ žestókuju <b>rasprávu</b> nad plénnymi krasnoarméjcami. Búdto by po tvojemú prikázu uničtóženy — sirečʹ porubany — trídcatʹ krasnoarméjcev, vzjátyje Xarlampijem Jermakovym pod Bókovskoj. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>”</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Much esteemed Comrade Grigory Panteleyevich, Wicked rumours are reaching our ears that you are allegedly meting out <b>brutal treatment</b> to captured Red Army men. It is said that on your orders thirty Red prisoners captured by Kharlampy Yermakov at Bokovskaya were destroyed, that is to say, cut to pieces. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>short work</li></ol>

***расправить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расправить.html>распра́вить</a> (11653)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>пра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправить.html>распра́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasprávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправлять.html>расправля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smooth out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расправить.html>распра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:складка.html>скла́дки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasprávitʹ</b> skládki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to smooth out creases</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расправить.html>распра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:морщина.html>морщи́ны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лоб.html>лбу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasprávitʹ</b> morščíny na lbu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unknit the brow</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to straighten, to stretch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расправить.html>распра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плечо.html>пле́чи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasprávitʹ</b> pléči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to straighten/square one's shoulders</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расправить.html>распра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>кры́лья</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasprávitʹ</b> krýlʹja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spread/stretch one's wings</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***расправиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расправиться.html>распра́виться</a> (9861)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправить.html>распра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasprávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправиться.html>распра́виться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasprávitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправляться.html>расправля́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to beat violently, to punish</li>
<li>to get rid of (someone) by destroying them or rendering them harmless</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deal with (something), to handle (something), to manage (something)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расправиться.html>распра́виться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:суд.html>суда́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasprávitʹsja</b> bez sudá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take the law into one's own hands</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eat up (something) without leaving a trace</li>
<li>to get smoothed out, to even out</li>
<li>to become straight, to straighten out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плечо.html>пле́чи</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:расправиться.html>распра́вились</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pléči <b>rasprávilisʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">one's shoulders <b>straightened up</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправить.html>распра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasprávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***расправлявший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расправлять.html>расправля́вший</a> (17584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправлять.html>расправля́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspravljávšij</span>)

***расправлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расправлять.html>расправля́ть</a> (17584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправить.html>распра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasprávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправлять.html>расправля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspravljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправить.html>распра́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smooth out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расправлять.html>расправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:складка.html>скла́дки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspravljátʹ</b> skládki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to smooth out creases</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расправлять.html>расправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:морщина.html>морщи́ны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лоб.html>лбу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspravljátʹ</b> morščíny na lbu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unknit the brow</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to straighten, to stretch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расправлять.html>расправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плечо.html>пле́чи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspravljátʹ</b> pléči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to straighten/square one's shoulders</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расправлять.html>расправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>кры́лья</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspravljátʹ</b> krýlʹja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spread/stretch one's wings</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***расправляться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расправляться.html>расправля́ться</a> (15958)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправлять.html>расправля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspravljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправляться.html>расправля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspravljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправиться.html>распра́виться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to beat violently, to punish</li>
<li>to get rid of (someone) by destroying them or rendering them harmless</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deal with (something), to handle (something), to manage (something)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расправляться.html>расправля́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:суд.html>суда́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspravljátʹsja</b> bez sudá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take the law into one's own hands</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eat up (something) without leaving a trace</li>
<li>to get smoothed out, to even out</li>
<li>to become straight, to straighten out</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расправлять.html>расправля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspravljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***распределение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:распределение.html>распределе́ние</a> (6012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распределить.html>распредели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspredelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распределение.html>распределе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspredelénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распределение.html>распределе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распределение.html>распределе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распределение.html>распределе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>distribution <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act of distribution or being distributed</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равномерный.html>равноме́рное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:распределение.html>распределе́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ravnomérnoje <b>raspredelénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">even / uniform distribution</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>allocation (<i>e.g. of resources</i>)</li>
<li>assignment (<i>e.g. of young specialists by educational institutions</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приехать.html>прие́хала</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:распределение.html>распределе́нию</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná k nam prijéxala po <b>raspredeléniju</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">she came to us as her assignment <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">i.e. she was assigned to work at some place after graduating</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распроданный.html>распро́данный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspródannyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:распространение.html>распростране́ние</a> (4950)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распространить.html>распространи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasprostranítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распространение.html>распростране́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasprostranénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распространение.html>распростране́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распространение.html>распростране́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распространение.html>распростране́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>spread, expansion
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распространение.html>распростране́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вирус.html>ви́руса</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasprostranénije</b> vírusa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the spread of the virus</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>distribution, circulation</li>
<li>dissemination, propagation, spreading, distribution</li>
<li>prevalence, ubiquitousness</li></ol>
